(23 more)\n  \"Sujawal\"\n]\n\nfor district in districts:\n    for year in range(2000, 2026):\n        for case_status in [\"Pending\", \"Disposal\", \"All\"]:\n            search(district, year_from=year, year_to=year, case_status)\n            sleep(2)  # Rate limiting\n```\n\n### D. Search Results Table Structure\n\n**Table Endpoint**: Form submission returns HTML table\n\n**Result Table Format**:\n```\n<table>\n  <thead>\n    <tr>\n      <th>S.No</th>\n      <th>Case No</th>\n      <th>Court Name</th>\n      <th>Status</th>\n      <th>Hearing Date</th>\n      <th>Action</th>\n    </tr>\n  </thead>\n  <tbody>\n    <tr>\n      <td>1</td>\n      <td>Criminal Bail Application 2020/2024, Shehzad Ghulam Hussain son of Ghulam Hussain V/S The State</td>\n      <td>Additional District & Sessions Judge XI, Karachi (South)</td>\n      <td>Disposed 04/Jul/2024</td>\n      <td>04/Jul/2024</td>\n      <td>\n        <button onclick=\"viewCase(...)\">View</button>\n        OR\n        \"NOT FOUND\" (text)\n      </td>\n    </tr>\n    <!-- More rows -->\n  </tbody>\n</table>\n```\n\n**Data Extraction Pattern**:\n```python\n# For each row in results table:\nrow = {\n    \"s_no\": cell_0_text,\n    \"case_no\": cell_1_text,              # EXTRACT: All case details\n    \"court_name\": cell_2_text,           # EXTRACT: Bench location\n    \"status\": cell_3_text,               # EXTRACT: Status & date\n    \"hearing_date\": cell_4_text,         # EXTRACT: Next hearing\n    \"action_url\": cell_5_button_onclick, # EXTRACT: Case detail link (if exists)\n    \"case_available\": cell_5_text != \"NOT FOUND\"\n}\n\n# Parse case_no field for details:\npattern = r\"(\\w+)\\s+(\\d{4})/(\\d{4}),\\s+(.+?)\\s+V/S\\s+(.+)\"\nmatch = re.search(pattern, row[\"case_no\"])\nif match:\n    case_type, year_filed, year_current, plaintiff, defendant = match.groups()\n```\n\n### G. Case Detail Page Structure\n\n**Detail URL Pattern**:\n- Not directly visible in search results\n- \"NOT FOUND\" text indicates page doesn't exist in database\n- When available: Click \"Action\" button returns case details\n\n**Expected Detail Page Fields** (when available):\n```\nCase Information:\n  - Case Number (full)\n  - Case Type\n  - Year Filed\n  - Court Jurisdiction\n  - Judge Name\n  - Court Location/Bench\n\nParties:\n  - Plaintiff/Petitioner Name(s)\n  - Plaintiff Address\n  - Defendant/Respondent Name(s)\n  - Defendant Address\n  - Counsel Names (if available)\n\nCase Details:\n  - FIR Number (criminal cases)\n  - Statement of Facts\n  - Charges/Claims\n  - Pleas/Defenses\n  - Evidence Summary\n\nOrders/Judgment:\n  - Hearing Dates\n  - Interim Orders\n  - Final Judgment/Disposal Date\n  - Judge's Findings\n  - Judgment Text (if digitized)\n\nCase Status:\n  - Current Status (Pending/Disposed)\n  - Last Updated Date\n  - Next Hearing Date (if pending)\n```\n\n### H. Pagination Strategy\n\n**Observation**: Not visible in initial snapshots, but likely present\n\n**Expected Pagination**:\n- Search results return 10-20 cases per page\n- Pagination controls appear at bottom of table\n- Standard patterns: \"Next\", \"Previous\", page numbers, or \"Load More\"\n\n**Crawler Approach**:\n```python\n# After initial search, check for pagination\ndef handle_pagination(page_html):\n    # Look for:\n    # - Next button (class: 'pagination-next', 'next-page', etc.)\n    # - Page numbers\n    # - \"Load More\" button\n    # - Pagination info: \"Showing 1-20 of 500\"\n\n    next_page_url = extract_next_page_link(page_html)\n    while next_page_url:\n        results.extend(parse_results(fetch(next_page_url)))\n        sleep(1)  # Rate limit\n        next_page_url = extract_next_page_link(last_response)\n```\n\n### I. Data Quality & Anomalies\n\n**Known Issues**:\n1. **Incomplete Digitization**: 80% of cases return \"NOT FOUND\" on detail page\n2. **Party Names**: May contain Urdu characters (Unicode handling required)\n3. **Court Names**: Format varies (e.g., \"Additional District & Sessions Judge XI\" vs variations)\n4. **Date Parsing**: Multiple formats observed (DD/Mon/YYYY, YYYY-MM-DD)\n5. **Duplicate Cases**: Same case may appear in multiple districts (concurrent jurisdiction)\n\n**Handling Strategy**:\n```python\n# Character encoding\nresponse.encoding = 'utf-8'\ncase_data = {\n    'plaintiff': clean_unicode(plaintiff_text),\n    'defendant': clean_unicode(defendant_text)\n}\n\n# Date parsing\nimport dateutil.parser\nhearing_date = dateutil.parser.parse(hearing_date_string)\n\n# Deduplication\ncase_id = hashlib.md5(\n    f\"{case_no}|{court_name}|{year_filed}\".encode()\n).hexdigest()\n```\n\n### J. Crawl4AI Configuration\n\n**Crawl4AI Strategy Block**:\n```yaml\nstrategy:\n  type: \"form-based\"\n  crawl_delay: 2  # seconds between requests\n  rate_limit:\n    per_minute: 30\n    per_hour: 1000\n\n  search_patterns:\n    - district: [all 27]\n    - year_from: [2000-2025]\n    - case_status: [\"All\", \"Pending\", \"Disposal\"]\n    - case_category: [\"All\"]  # Start with \"All\", expand if needed\n\n  extraction:\n    - selector: \"table tbody tr\"\n      fields:\n        - s_no: \"td:nth-child(1)\"\n        - case_no: \"td:nth-child(2)\"\n        - court_name: \"td:nth-child(3)\"\n        - status: \"td:nth-child(4)\"\n        - hearing_date: \"td:nth-child(5)\"\n        - detail_link: \"td:nth-child(6) button@onclick\"\n\n  pagination:\n    - detect: \"next_page_link\"\n    - follow: true\n    - max_pages: unlimited\n    - wait_between_pages: 2000  # milliseconds\n\nerror_handling:\n  - retry_failed: true\n  - retry_count: 3\n  - skip_not_found: true\n  - log_failures: true\n```\n\n### K. Expected Data Volume\n\n**Estimation**:\n- **Total Records**: 500,000 - 2,000,000 cases\n- **By Scope**:\n  - Karachi alone: ~100,000 cases/year × 10-20 years = 1,000,000+\n  - All 27 districts: 2,000,000+ cases (conservative)\n- **Digitized Judgments**: 10% available = 50,000-100,000 PDFs\n- **Crawl Time**: 100-200 hours for complete extraction (with 2-sec delays)\n\n**Storage Requirements**:\n- Metadata only: ~500 MB (JSON records)\n- With PDFs: 50-200 GB (assuming avg 2-5 MB per PDF)\n- Database (SQLite/PostgreSQL): 1-2 GB\n\n---\n\n## TIER 2: digital.shc.gov.pk Specification\n\n### A. Entry Point\n\n**Base URL**: `https://digital.shc.gov.pk/`\n\n**Robots.txt**:\n```\nUser-agent: *\nDisallow:\n```\n✓ Fully crawlable\n\n**Navigation**:\n```\nGET https://digital.shc.gov.pk/\n  └─ /search-citation (citation-based case law search)\n  └─ /advocate/register (registration - skip)\n  └─ /login (authentication - skip public crawl)\n```\n\n### B. Citation Search Form\n\n**Endpoint**: POST `https://digital.shc.gov.pk/search-citation`\n\n**Form Fields**:\n```\ncitation_year : string (YYYY, required)\njournal        : string (dropdown, required)\njournal_part   : string (dropdown, depends on journal, optional)\npage_no        : string (integer, optional)\n```\n\n**Journal Options** (21 total):\n```\nSHC             - Sindh High Court Reports\nPLD             - Pakistan Legal Decisions\nSCMR            - Supreme Court Monthly Review\nCLC             - Commercial Law Cases\nPCr.LJ          - Pakistan Criminal Law Journal\nPTD             - Pakistan Tax Decisions\nPLC             - Pakistan Law Cases\nCLD             - Constitutional Law Decisions\nYLR             - Yearly Law Reports\nOTHER           - Miscellaneous journals\n\nSBLR            - Sindh Bar Law Reports\nMLD             - Muslim Law Decisions\nPSC             - Pakistan Supreme Court\nTAX             - Tax Reports\nNLR             - National Law Reports\nAC              - Appeals Cases\nCLJ             - Commercial Law Journal\nSD              - Sindh Digest\nTD              - Tax Digest\nUC              - Unreported Cases\nPLJ             - Pakistan Law Journal\n\nSLJ, SLR        - Sindh Law Reports\nPCr.R           - Pakistan Criminal Reports\nPTCL            - Pakistan Telecom Law\nPLC (CS)        - PLC Computer Science\n```\n\n### C. Search Strategy\n\n**Challenge**: Citation-based search requires knowing case citation in advance\n\n**Possible Crawler Approaches**:\n\n**Option 1 - Brute Force** (Recommended):\n```python\njournals = [\"SHC\", \"PLD\", \"SCMR\", \"CLC\", ...]\nyears = range(2000, 2026)\npage_ranges = range(1, 5000)  # Estimate max pages per journal per year\n\nfor journal in journals:\n    for year in years:\n        for page in page_ranges:\n            search_params = {\n                'citation_year': year,\n                'journal': journal,\n                'page_no': page\n            }\n            result = search(search_params)\n            if result.has_data:\n                extract_case(result)\n            else:\n                break  # No more pages for this journal/year\n            sleep(2)  # Rate limit\n```\n\n**Option 2 - Intelligent Extraction**:\n```python\n# From Tier 1 results, extract citations\nfor case in tier1_results:\n    if case.has_citation:\n        citation = parse_citation(case.citation)\n        search(citation.year, citation.journal, citation.page)\n        sleep(2)\n```\n\n### D. Search Results Structure\n\n**Expected Result Format** (citation lookup):\n```\nCase Citation:\n  Year: 2023\n  Journal: SHC (Sindh High Court)\n  Page: 152\n\nCase Information:\n  Title: Plaintiff v/s Defendant\n  Case Number: [Full case ID]\n  Judge: Hon'ble Justice [Name]\n  Judgment Date: DD/MM/YYYY\n\nFull Text: [HTML or PDF link]\nPDF Download: [Direct link to PDF]\n```\n\n### E. reCAPTCHA Handling\n\n**Observed**: reCAPTCHA v3/v2 present on page (iframe element detected)\n\n**Mitigation Strategies**:\n1. **reCAPTCHA Solver Service**:\n   - 2Captcha (https://2captcha.com) - $0.001-0.003 per solve\n   - Anti-Captcha (https://anti-captcha.com)\n   - CapMonster (https://capmonster.cloud)\n\n2. **Request Patterns**:\n   - Space requests 5+ seconds apart\n   - Rotate user agents\n   - Vary request origins (rotating proxies)\n   - Implement exponential backoff on CAPTCHA triggers\n\n3. **Code Example**:\n```python\nfrom crawl4ai import AsyncWebCrawler\nfrom twocaptcha import TwoCaptcha\n\nasync def search_with_captcha(search_params):\n    async with AsyncWebCrawler() as crawler:\n        # Initial request\n        response = await crawler.arun(\n            url=\"https://digital.shc.gov.pk/search-citation\",\n            bypass_cache=True,\n            user_agent=\"Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)\"\n        )\n\n        # If CAPTCHA detected\n        if \"g-recaptcha\" in response.html:\n            # Solve CAPTCHA\n            solver = TwoCaptcha(apikey=\"YOUR_KEY\")\n            result = solver.recaptcha(\n                sitekey=\"6LE...\",\n                url=\"https://digital.shc.gov.pk/search-citation\"\n            )\n\n            # Submit form with token\n            await crawler.arun(\n                url=\"https://digital.shc.gov.pk/search-citation\",\n                method=\"POST\",\n                data={\n                    **search_params,\n                    'g-recaptcha-response': result\n                }\n            )\n```\n\n### F. ON CONFLICT (district, year_start, year_end, case_status) DO UPDATE SET\n                    records_found = $5,\n                    updated_at = NOW()\n            \"\"\", district, year_start, year_end, case_status, records_found)\n\n# ============================================================================\n# CASE DATA EXTRACTION\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass CaseExtractor:\n    \"\"\"Extract case data from search results\"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def parse_case_number(case_no_text: str) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse case number string into components.\n\n        Format: \"CaseType YYYY/YYYY, Plaintiff V/S Defendant\"\n        Example: \"Criminal Bail Application 2020/2024, Shehzad Ghulam Hussain\n                  son of Ghulam Hussain V/S The State\"\n        \"\"\"\n        import re\n\n        case_data = {\n            'case_number': case_no_text,\n            'case_type': None,\n            'year_filed': None,\n            'plaintiff': None,\n            'defendant': None,\n        }\n\n        # Pattern: CaseType YYYY/YYYY, Parties\n        pattern = r\"^(.+?)\\s+(\\d{4})/(\\d{4}),\\s+(.+?)\\s+V/S\\s+(.+)$\"\n        match = re.search(pattern, case_no_text.strip())\n\n        if match:\n            case_data['case_type'] = match.group(1).strip()\n            case_data['year_filed'] = int(match.group(2))\n            case_data['plaintiff'] = match.group(4).strip()\n            case_data['defendant'] = match.group(5).strip()\n\n        return case_data\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def parse_court_name(court_name_text: str) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse court name to extract judge and bench location.\n\n        Format: \"Judge Title, District (Subdivision)\"\n        \"\"\"\n        import re\n\n        court_data = {\n            'court_name': court_name_text,\n            'judge_name': None,\n            'bench_location': None,\n        }\n\n        # Try to extract judge title (before comma)\n        parts = court_name_text.split(',')\n        if len(parts) >= 1:\n            court_data['judge_name'] = parts[0].strip()\n\n        # Extract location (in parentheses)\n        location_match = re.search(r'\\(([^)]+)\\)', court_name_text)\n        if location_match:\n            court_data['bench_location'] = location_match.group(1).strip()\n\n        return court_data\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def parse_status(status_text: str) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse status field to extract current status and dates.\n\n        Formats:\n        - \"Disposed 04/Jul/2024\"\n        - \"Pending\"\n        - \"Adjourned to 15/Mar/2026\"\n        \"\"\"\n        import re\n\n        status_data = {\n            'current_status': None,\n            'disposal_date': None,\n            'hearing_date': None,\n        }\n\n        if 'Disposed' in status_text:\n            status_data['current_status'] = 'Disposed'\n            # Extract date\n            date_match = re.search(r'(\\d{2}/\\w+/\\d{4})', status_text)\n            if date_match:\n                try:\n                    status_data['disposal_date'] = dateutil.parser.parse(\n                        date_match.group(1),\n                        dayfirst=True\n                    ).isoformat()\n                except:\n                    status_data['disposal_date'] = date_match.group(1)\n\n        elif 'Pending' in status_text:\n            status_data['current_status'] = 'Pending'\n\n        elif 'Adjourned' in status_text:\n            status_data['current_status'] = 'Adjourned'\n            # Extract next hearing date\n            date_match = re.search(r'(\\d{2}/\\w+/\\d{4})', status_text)\n            if date_match:\n                try:\n                    status_data['hearing_date'] = dateutil.parser.parse(\n                        date_match.group(1),\n                        dayfirst=True\n                    ).isoformat()\n                except:\n                    status_data['hearing_date'] = date_match.group(1)\n\n        return status_data\n\n    @classmethod\n    def extract_from_table_row(cls, row_html: str, district: str) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Extract case data from a table row.\n\n        Returns dict with all case fields or None if parse fails.\n        \"\"\"\n        try:\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(row_html, 'html.parser')\n            cells = soup.find_all('td')\n\n            if len(cells) < 6:\n                return None\n\n            # Extract cell contents\n            s_no = cells[0].get_text(strip=True)\n            case_no_text = cells[1].get_text(strip=True)\n            court_name_text = cells[2].get_text(strip=True)\n            status_text = cells[3].get_text(strip=True)\n            hearing_date_text = cells[4].get_text(strip=True)\n\n            # Check if document available\n            action_cell = cells[5].get_text(strip=True)\n            document_available = \"NOT FOUND\" not in action_cell\n\n            # Parse components\n            case_parts = cls.parse_case_number(case_no_text)\n            court_parts = cls.parse_court_name(court_name_text)\n            status_parts = cls.parse_status(status_text)\n\n            # Create case ID hash for deduplication\n            case_id_hash = hashlib.md5(\n                f\"{case_no_text}|{court_name_text}|{district}\".encode()\n            ).hexdigest()\n\n            # Merge all data\n            case_data = {\n                'case_id_hash': case_id_hash,\n                'district': district,\n                'document_available': document_available,\n                **case_parts,\n                **court_parts,\n                **status_parts,\n            }\n\n            # Add hearing date if in status\n            if hearing_date_text and not case_data.get('hearing_date'):\n                try:\n                    case_data['hearing_date'] = dateutil.parser.parse(\n                        hearing_date_text,\n                        dayfirst=True\n                    ).isoformat()\n                except:\n                    case_data['hearing_date'] = hearing_date_text\n\n            return case_data\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error parsing table row: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n# ============================================================================\n# CRAWLER\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass SindhCourtsC rawler:\n    \"\"\"Main crawler orchestrator\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, db_url: str):\n        self.db = DatabaseManager(db_url)\n        self.extractor = CaseExtractor()\n        self.session = None\n        self.request_times = []  # Track request timing for rate limiting\n\n    async def init(self):\n        \"\"\"Initialize crawler\"\"\"\n        await self.db.connect()\n        self.session = aiohttp.ClientSession()\n        logger.info(\"Crawler initialized\")\n\n    async def close(self):\n        \"\"\"Cleanup\"\"\"\n        await self.db.disconnect()\n        if self.session:\n            await self.session.close()\n\n    async def _rate_limit(self):\n        \"\"\"Implement rate limiting (30 req/min = 1 req/2 sec)\"\"\"\n        await asyncio.sleep(CRAWL_DELAY)\n\n    async def _search_cases(\n        self,\n        district: str,\n        year_from: int,\n        year_to: int,\n        case_status: str = \"All\"\n    ) -> Optional[CrawlResult]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute search request.\n\n        Returns raw HTML result from Crawl4AI or None on failure.\n        \"\"\"\n        await self._rate_limit()\n\n        search_params = {\n            'district': district,\n            'year_from': year_from,\n            'year_to': year_to,\n            'case_status': case_status,\n            'court_type': 'NIL-Default Court Type',\n            'case_category': 'All',\n        }\n\n        logger.info(\n            f\"Searching: {district} | {year_from}-{year_to} | {case_status}\"\n        )\n\n        retry_count = 0\n        while retry_count < MAX_RETRIES:\n            try:\n                async with AsyncWebCrawler() as crawler:\n                    result = await crawler.arun(\n                        url=SEARCH_ENDPOINT,\n                        method=\"GET\",\n                        params=search_params,\n                        wait_for=\"table tbody\",\n                        timeout=REQUEST_TIMEOUT,\n                        user_agent=\"Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36\"\n                    )\n\n                    if result.status_code == 200:\n                        return result\n\n                    logger.warning(\n                        f\"Search returned status {result.status_code}. \"\n                        f\"Retry {retry_count + 1}/{MAX_RETRIES}\"\n                    )\n\n            except asyncio.TimeoutError:\n                logger.warning(f\"Timeout during search. Retry {retry_count + 1}/{MAX_RETRIES}\")\n\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f\"Error during search: {e}. Retry {retry_count + 1}/{MAX_RETRIES}\")\n\n            retry_count += 1\n            if retry_count < MAX_RETRIES:\n                await asyncio.sleep(CRAWL_DELAY * (RETRY_BACKOFF ** retry_count))\n\n        return None\n\n    async def _extract_results(self, html: str, district: str) -> List[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Extract all cases from result HTML.\n\n        Uses BeautifulSoup to parse table structure.\n        \"\"\"\n        cases = []\n        try:\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')\n            table = soup.find('table')\n\n            if not table:\n                logger.warning(f\"No table found for {district}\")\n                return cases\n\n            tbody = table.find('tbody')\n            if not tbody:\n                logger.warning(f\"No tbody found in table for {district}\")\n                return cases\n\n            rows = tbody.find_all('tr')\n            logger.info(f\"Found {len(rows)} rows for {district}\")\n\n            for row in rows:\n                case = self.extractor.extract_from_table_row(str(row), district)\n                if case:\n                    cases.append(case)\n\n            return cases\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error extracting results: {e}\")\n            return cases\n\n    async def crawl_district_year(\n        self,\n        district: str,\n        year_from: int,\n        year_to: int,\n        case_status: str\n    ) -> Tuple[int, int]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Crawl single district/year/status combination.\n\n        Returns (records_found, records_inserted).\n        \"\"\"\n        logger.info(f\"Crawling: {district} ({year_from}-{year_to}) {case_status}\")\n\n        result = await self._search_cases(district, year_from, year_to, case_status)\n\n        if not result:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to fetch results for {district}\")\n            return (0, 0)\n\n        cases = await self._extract_results(result.html, district)\n        inserted = 0\n\n        for case in cases:\n            if await self.db.insert_case(case):\n                inserted += 1\n\n        logger.info(\n            f\"District complete: {district} | Found: {len(cases)} | \"\n            f\"Inserted: {inserted}\"\n        )\n\n        return (len(cases), inserted)\n\n    async def crawl_all(\n        self,\n        start_year: int = 2000,\n        end_year: int = 2025\n    ) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute full crawl of all districts and years.\n\n        Returns summary statistics.\n        \"\"\"\n        logger.info(\"Starting full crawl\")\n        stats = {\n            'total_cases_found': 0,\n            'total_cases_inserted': 0,\n            'total_errors': 0,\n            'start_time': datetime.now(),\n        }\n\n        tasks = []\n\n        for district in DISTRICTS:\n            for year in range(start_year, end_year + 1):\n                for status in CASE_STATUS_OPTIONS:\n                    # Create task for each search combination\n                    task = self.crawl_district_year(district, year, year, status)\n                    tasks.append(task)\n\n        # Execute tasks with concurrency limit (5 concurrent)\n        semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(5)\n\n        async def bounded_task(task):\n            async with semaphore:\n                return await task\n\n        results = await asyncio.gather(*[bounded_task(t) for t in tasks], return_exceptions=True)\n\n        for result in results:\n            if isinstance(result, tuple):\n                stats['total_cases_found'] += result[0]\n                stats['total_cases_inserted'] += result[1]\n            elif isinstance(result, Exception):\n                logger.error(f\"Task error: {result}\")\n                stats['total_errors'] += 1\n\n        stats['end_time'] = datetime.now()\n        stats['duration_hours'] = (\n            stats['end_time'] - stats['start_time']\n        ).total_seconds() / 3600\n\n        logger.info(f\"Crawl complete: {json.dumps(stats, default=str, indent=2)}\")\n        return stats\n\n#
